context validation in Kubernetes is implemented across two main components:\\n\\n1. **Admission Control Layer**: The PodSecurity admission controller (staging/src/k8s.io/pod-security-admission/) implements pod security standards validation through policy checks that enforce restricted and baseline policies.\\n\\n2. **Core Validation**: The kubernetes API validation layer (pkg/apis/core/validation/validation.go) provides field-level validation for security context attributes.\\n\\n**RunAsNonRoot Enforcement** is validated in check_runAsNonRoot.go which implements the CheckRunAsNonRoot() function and its corresponding runAsNonRoot_1_0() check function. Baseline allows runtime/default, docker/default, or localhost profiles.\\n- Restricted level: check_seccompProfile_restricted.go implements CheckSeccompProfileRestricted() which requires a seccomp profile to be set and only allows RuntimeDefault or Localhost types.\\n\\n**Core API Validation** in pkg/apis/core/validation/validation.go implements:\\n- ValidateSecurityContext(): validates SecurityContext fields including privileged flag and capabilities restrictions\\n- validateSeccompProfileField(): validates seccomp profile configuration\\n- validatePodSpecSecurityContext(): validates pod-level security context including seccomp profiles\\n\\nThese validation layers work together to enforce Kubernetes Pod Security Standards through the admission controller plugin (plugin/pkg/admission/security/podsecurity/admission.go) which delegates to the upstream pod-security-admission library (staging/src/k8s.io/pod-security-admission/) for policy evaluation and enforcement.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":64,"cache_creation_input_tokens":2671,"cache_read_input_tokens":57673,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":2671},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"8ddaeb58-c391-409d-8af7-586596750cb1","uuid":"06805a76-1be4-4304-95f2-e66686ce3a25"}
